Users can easily enjoy genuine Asian calligraphy and ink wash painting with a simple and intuitive user interface imbued with the Zen spirit.\r\n\r\nThe Windows universal app version of Zen Brush 2 already supports the Surface Dial and the new Surface Pen with tilt support, providing the feeling of a real ink brush by reflecting the brush's tilt and orientation.\r\n\r\nMain Features :\r\n\r\n■3D Ink Brush Simulation\r\nThe app includes a drawing system based on a 3D model of an East Asian ink brush. Reihenfolge oder nach Kapiteln sortiert.\r\n•Statistik: Übersichtliche Trainingsstände zu einzelnen Kapiteln des Schulbuchs - so behältst du deinen Lernfortschritt stets im Blick.\r\n•Spiel-Modus:
